<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="color:windowtext;font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-decoration:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Items 1.01 and 2.01&#160; Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement
and Completion of Acquisition or Disposition of Assets.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On December&nbsp;17, 2004, Perficient, Inc.
(the &#147;Perficient&#148;), Perficient ZettaWorks, Inc., a Delaware corporation and a
wholly -owned subsidiary of Perficient (the &#147;Acquisition Sub&#148;) and ZettaWorks
LLC (&#147;ZettaWorks&#148;), a Texas limited liability company, entered into an Asset
Purchase Agreement (the &#147;Purchase Agreement&#148;) pursuant to which Acquisition Sub
acquired substantially all of the assets and assumed certain liabilities of
ZettaWorks (the &#147;Acquisition&#148;).&#160; The
Acquisition closed on December&nbsp;20, 2004.&#160;
The total consideration paid in the Acquisition is $10.7&#160; million, which amount includes approximately
$2.9 million in cash and up to $7.8 million worth of Perficient&#146;s common stock,
based on the average closing price of Perficient&#146;s common stock for the three
trading days immediately preceding the acquisition, which amount remains
subject to certain post-closing adjustments.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The operating management of ZettaWorks will
receive only Perficient common stock and Perficient stock options in the
transaction.&#160; The Purchase Agreement
includes other terms and provisions of the type customary in agreements of this
sort.&#160; The assets acquired in the
Acquisition include accounts receivable, personal property, intellectual
property rights, the rights and benefits under certain contracts and intangible
assets relating to the business of ZettaWorks.&#160;
Prior to the Acquisition, the assets of ZettaWorks were used to provide
information technology consulting services to its customers.&#160; Perficient intends to continue such uses for
the assets of ZettaWorks.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The foregoing summary does not purport to be complete and is qualified
in its entirety by reference to the full text of the</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Purchase Agreement, a copy of which is included herein
as Exhibit 2.1.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The press release announcing the acquisition is included herein as
Exhibit 99.1 to this Form 8-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item
9.01 Financial Statements and Exhibits</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(a)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Financial Statements of
Business Acquired</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Financial Statements relating to the acquisition
described in this Form 8-K and required pursuant to Rule 3-05 of Regulation S-X
are not included herein but will be filed by an amendment to this Form 8-K
within seventy-one (71) days from December&nbsp;23, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(b)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pro Forma Financial
Information</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma financial information relating to the
acquisitions described in this Form 8-K and required pursuant to Article&nbsp;11
of Regulation S-X are not included herein but will be filed by an amendment to
this Form 8-K within seventy-one (71) days from December&nbsp;23, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(c)</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibits</font></b></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;text-decoration:underline;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ASSET PURCHASE AGREEMENT </font></u></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ASSET
PURCHASE AGREEMENT (the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Agreement</i></b></font>&#148;) dated
as of December 17, 2004, by and among Perficient, Inc., a Delaware corporation
(&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Parent</i></b></font>&#148;), Perficient
ZettaWorks, Inc., a Delaware corporation and a wholly owned subsidiary of
Parent (&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Buyer</i></b></font>&#148;), and ZettaWorks, LLC,
a Texas limited liability company (the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Seller</i></b></font>&#148;).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in 6.0pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Seller is engaged in the business of
providing business and information systems consulting services and staffing for
customers (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Business</font></i></b>&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Buyer
desires to purchase from Seller, and Seller desires to sell to Buyer,
substantially all of Seller&#146;s assets and properties used or held for use in
connection with the Business, and in connection therewith, Buyer has agreed to
assume certain of the liabilities of Seller relating to the Business, all on
the terms and conditions set forth herein (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Acquisition</font></i></b>&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOW,
THEREFORE, in consideration of the mutual covenants, representations,
warranties and agreements contained herein, and intending to be legally bound
hereby, the parties agree as follows:</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="ArticleIDefinitions"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ARTICLE I</font></b></a><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;"><br>
</font></b></font><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">DEFINITIONS</font></b></font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">1.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="Definitions">Definitions</a></font></b>.&#160; As used in this Agreement, the following
terms shall have the meanings set forth or referenced below:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Accounts Receivable</font></i></b>&#148; means any and all
accounts receivable and notes receivable of or amounts owing or payable to
Seller, including costs and estimated earnings in excess of billings related to
the Seller&#146;s work in progress, all as of the Closing Date.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Ancillary Agreements</font></i></b>&#148; means the Escrow
Agreement, the Agreement and Bill of Sale, and the Transition Services
Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Assets</font></i></b>&#148; means all the tangible and
intangible assets owned, leased, or licensed by Seller that are used or held
for use in connection with the Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Business Records</font></i></b>&#148; means any and all
books, records, files, documentation, data or information of seller that have
been or now are used in connection with the Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Choses in Action</font></i></b>&#148; means a right to
receive or recover property, debt, or damages on a cause of action, whether
pending or not and whether arising in contract, tort or otherwise.&#160; The term shall include rights to
indemnification, damages for breach of warranty or any other event or
circumstance, judgments, settlements, and proceeds from judgments or
settlements.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Code</font></i></b>&#148; means the United States Internal
Revenue Code of 1986, as amended.&#160; All
references to the Code, U.S. Treasury regulations or other governmental
pronouncements shall be deemed to include references to any applicable
successor regulations or amending pronouncement.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>

<div align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Commonly Controlled Entity</font></i></b>&#148; means any
corporation, trade, business, or entity under common control with the Seller,
within the meaning of Section 414(b), (c), (m), or (o) of the Code or Section
4001 of ERISA.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Competing
Business</i></b></font>&#148; means any person, entity, or other business concern
that offers or is planning to offer Competitive Products or Services.&#160; A person, entity, or other business concern
that offers or plans to offer Competitive Products or Services and also offers
or plans to offer other services is considered a Competing Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Competitive
Products or Services</i></b></font>&#148; means:&#160;
(i) providing, as a primary business, technology consulting services,
technology design services, systems integration services, technology
outsourcing services, hosting services or technology staffing services; and
(ii) products or services that are otherwise competitive with any of the
products or services being offered, marketed, or actively developed (as
evidenced by internal company documents and records, including e-mail) by the
Parent or Buyer as of the beginning of the Noncompetition Period.&#160; For the avoidance of doubt, the design,
development, manufacture, distribution and marketing of computer software
products for resale and/or licensing to commercial and retail customers shall
not be considered &#147;Competitive Products or Services&#148; for purposes of this
Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Consents</font></i></b>&#148; means all consents and
approvals of third parties or Governmental Entities, in each case that are
necessary in order to transfer the Acquired Assets to Buyer and otherwise to
consummate the transactions contemplated hereby.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Contracts</font></i></b>&#148; means all written or oral
contracts, agreements, leases, licenses and other arrangements pursuant to
which Seller enjoys any right or benefit or undertakes any obligation related
to the Business or otherwise.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Covered
Client</i></b></font>&#148; means:&#160; (i) any of
the Parent&#146;s, Buyer&#146;s or Seller&#146;s clients or Prospective Clients.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Current Employee Benefit Plan</font></i></b>&#148; means
each Employee Benefit Plan that is currently sponsored, maintained, contributed
to, or agreed to by the Seller or any Commonly Controlled Entity or under which
the Seller or any Commonly Controlled Entity has any current or future
obligations.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Employee Benefit Plan</font></i></b>&#148; means each (i)
employee benefit plan within the meaning of Section 3(3) of ERISA and (ii)
personnel policy; stock option plan; stock purchase plan; equity compensation
plan; phantom equity or appreciation rights plan; collective bargaining
agreement; bonus plan or arrangement; incentive award plan or arrangement;
vacation policy; severance pay plan, policy, or agreement; deferred
compensation agreement or arrangement; executive compensation or supplemental
income arrangement; consulting agreement; employment agreement; and other
employee benefit plan, agreement, arrangement, program, practice, or
understanding, which is sponsored, maintained,&#160;
contributed to, or agreed to by the Seller or any Commonly Controlled
Entity for the benefit of the employees, former employees, independent
contractors, or agents of the Seller or any Commonly Controlled Entity or has
been so sponsored, maintained, contributed to, or agreed to at any time within
six years prior to Closing Date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Encumbrances</font></i></b>&#148; means any and all
restrictions on or conditions to transfer or assignment, claims, liens,
pledges, mortgages, restrictions, and encumbrances of any kind, whether
accrued, absolute, contingent or otherwise affecting the Acquired Assets.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">&#147;<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">ERISA</font></b></font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#148;
means the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974, as amended.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Governmental
Entity</i></b></font>&#148; means any court, administrative agency, regulatory agency
or commission or other governmental authority or instrumentality.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Intellectual
Property Rights</i></b></font>&#148; means all patents, copyrights, trade secrets,
trade names, service marks, trademarks, domain names, know-how, software and
other intellectual property that is owned or licensed by Seller and used in
connection with the operation of the Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Liabilities</font></i></b>&#148;&#160; means any direct or indirect liability,
indebtedness, obligation, guarantee or endorsement, whether known or unknown,
whether accrued or unaccrued, whether absolute or contingent, whether due or to
become due, or whether liquidated or unliquidated, of Seller relating to the
Business or the Assets.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Net Working Capital</font></i></b>&#148; means the Accounts
Receivable (net of allowances for doubtful accounts) included in the Acquired
Assets, less the Assumed Liabilities identified on the Estimated Statement, as
revised by the Closing Date Statement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Noncompetition Period</font></i></b>&#148; means the period
beginning on the date hereof and ending on the second anniversary of the
Closing Date.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Parent Common Stock</font></i></b>&#148; means the Parent&#146;s
common stock, par value $0.001 per share.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Parent Stock Per Share Price</font></i></b>&#148; means the
average closing sale price of one share of Parent Common Stock as reported on
the Nasdaq SmallCap Market for the twenty&nbsp;(20) consecutive trading days
ending on the date that is one (1) trading day immediately preceding the
Closing Date (as adjusted as appropriate to reflect any stock splits, stock
dividends, combinations, reorganizations, reclassifications or similar events).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Permits</font></i></b>&#148; means all licenses, permits,
authorizations, certificates, franchises, variances, waivers, consents and
other approvals from any Governmental Entity relating to the operation of the
Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Permitted Encumbrances</font></i></b>&#148; means
(i)&nbsp;any Encumbrance for current Taxes that are not yet due or payable,
(ii)&nbsp;any Encumbrance for Tax assessments and other charges or claims with
respect to Taxes, the validity of which are being contested in good faith by
appropriate proceedings for which adequate reserves have been established in
accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, (iii)&nbsp;any minor
imperfection of title or similar Encumbrance which individually or in the
aggregate with other such Encumbrances does not impair the value of the
property subject to such Encumbrance or the use of such property in the conduct
of the business, (iv)&nbsp;mechanics&#146; and materialmen&#146;s liens incurred in the
ordinary course of business, (v)&nbsp;statutory liens of landlords&#146; and workmen&#146;s,
repairmen&#146;s, warehousemen&#146;s and carriers&#146; liens arising in the ordinary course
of business, (vi)&nbsp;requirements incurred or other Encumbrances relating to
deposits made in the ordinary course of business in connection with workers&#146;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Personal Property</font></i></b>&#148; means all of the
machinery, equipment, computer hardware, tools, motor vehicles, furniture,

office equipment, inventories, supplies, plant, spare parts, and other tangible

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Prospective

Buyer or Seller have spent time and resources courting or developing as a
potential user of the Parent&#146;s, the Buyer&#146;s or the Seller&#146;s Competitive
Products or Services as evidenced by internal company documents and records
(including e-mail); or (ii) has entered into specific discussions with the
Parent, the Buyer or the Seller regarding the Parent, the Buyer or the Seller
potentially providing its services or products to the person, entity, or
business concern.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Real Property</font></i></b><i><font style="font-style:italic;">&#148;</font></i> means all office facilities and other real property that
is owned or leased by Seller and used in connection with the operation of the
Business.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Restricted
Area</i></b></font>&#148; means any geographic market:&#160; (i) in which the Seller conducts any material
portion of the Business prior to the Closing Date; and/or (ii) in which the
Parent or Buyer was conducting business or actively pursuing a material amount
of business prior to the beginning of the Noncompetition Period as evidenced by
definite and demonstrable actions by the Parent or Buyer with respect to the
area (e.g., contacting clients or prospective clients to solicit material
selling business opportunities, contacting suppliers or vendors regarding
material business opportunities, actively conducting feasibility research of
the area, etc.).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Tax</i></b></font>&#148;
and &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Taxes</i></b></font>&#148; means any and all
taxes, charges, fees, levies or other assessments, including, without
limitation, all net income, gross income, gross receipts, premium, sales, use,
ad valorem, value added, transfer, franchise, profits, license, withholding,
payroll, employment, excise, estimated, severance, stamp, occupation, property
or other taxes, fees, assessments or charges of any kind whatsoever, together
with any interest and any penalties (including penalties for failure to file in
accordance with applicable information reporting requirements), and additions
to tax by any authority, whether federal, state, local, domestic or foreign.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Tax

document or information required to be supplied to any authority in connection
with Taxes.</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="ArticleIiSaleAndPurchaseOfAssets"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ARTICLE
II<br>
SALE AND PURCHASE OF ASSETS; ASSUMPTION OF LIABILITIES</font></b></a></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">2.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="AgreementToSellAndBuy">Agreement to Sell and Buy</a></font></b>.&#160; Subject to the terms and
conditions set forth in this Agreement, Seller shall sell, assign, transfer and
deliver to Buyer on the Closing Date, and Buyer shall purchase on the Closing
Date, all of Seller&#146;s right, title and interest in and to all of the Assets,
except the Excluded Assets set forth in <u>Section 2.02</u> (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Acquired Assets</font></i></b>&#148;),
free and clear of all Encumbrances other than Permitted Encumbrances.&#160; The Acquired Assets include the following:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; All Accounts Receivable;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; All Personal Property, including, to
the extent transferable, all rights and benefits of Seller under the lease
agreements listed on <u>Schedule 2.01(b)</u> (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Assigned Leases</font></i></b>&#148;);</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; All Intellectual Property Rights,
including, to the extent transferable, all rights and benefits of Seller under
the license agreements included on <u>Schedule 2.01(c)</u> (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Assigned Licenses</font></i></b>&#148;);</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 2.03&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="AssumptionOfLiabilities">Assumption of Liabilities</a></font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; As of the Closing Date, Buyer shall
assume and undertake to pay, perform and discharge according to their terms only
the following Liabilities of Seller (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Assumed
Liabilities</font></i></b>&#148;):</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities arising under the
Assigned Contracts from and after the Closing Date;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities reflected in the
Estimated Statement, as revised by the Closing Date Statement, including,
without limitation, (A) trade account payables, payroll related Taxes, 401(k)
matching contributions and other accruals arising in the ordinary course of
business that remain unpaid at and are not delinquent as of the Closing Date,
and (B) the obligation to provide products or to perform services relating to
billings in excess of costs or otherwise to be delivered or performed following
the Closing;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities related to any warranty
claims by Seller&#146;s customers with respect to work performed by Seller prior to
the Closing Date pursuant to any of the&#160;
Assigned Contracts (&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Seller Warranty Liabilities</font></i></b>&#148;); and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities listed on <u>Schedule 2.03</u>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Except as expressly set forth in <u>Section
2.03(a)</u> above, Buyer shall not assume or become liable or obligated in any
way, and Seller shall retain and remain solely liable for and obligated to pay,
perform and discharge all Liabilities of Seller, including, without limitation
any of the following (collectively, the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Excluded Liabilities</font></i></b>&#148;):</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities under any Contract other
than the Assigned Contracts;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Liabilities arising under the
Assigned Contracts that relate to the time period prior to the Closing Date or
arise out of events occurring prior to the Closing Date;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Any forfeiture, claim or pending
litigation or proceeding relating to the Business prior to the Closing Date;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Any Liabilities relating to unpaid
Taxes or to any Employee Benefit Plan or associated Contract.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 2.04&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="DeemedAssignmentOfContracts">Deemed Assignment of
Contracts</a>.</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; To the extent that the assignment hereunder
of any of the Assigned Contracts shall require the consent of any other party
(or in the event that any of the same shall be non-assignable), neither
this Agreement nor any actions taken hereunder shall constitute an assignment
or an agreement to assign if such assignment or attempted assignment would
constitute a breach thereof or result in a loss or diminution thereof;
provided, however, that Seller shall cooperate with Buyer to establish a
reasonable arrangement designed to provide Buyer with the benefits and burdens
of any Assigned Contract, including appointing Buyer to act as its agent to
perform all of Seller&#146;s obligations under such Assigned Contract and to collect
and promptly remit to Buyer all compensation received by Seller pursuant to
such Assigned Contract and, at Buyer&#146;s expense, to enforce, for the account and
benefit of Buyer, any</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">and all rights of Seller against
any other person arising out of the breach or cancellation of such Assigned
Contract by such other person or otherwise (any and all of which arrangements
shall constitute, as between the parties hereto, a deemed assignment or
transfer); provided, further, that Buyer shall undertake to pay or satisfy the
corresponding Liabilities under the terms of any such Assigned Contract to the
extent that Buyer would have been responsible therefor if such consent or
approval had been obtained and such Liability shall be deemed an Assumed
Liability for all purposes of this Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">2.05&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="PurchasePriceAndRelatedMatters">Purchase<font style="font-weight:bold;"><b> </b></font></a></font><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b>Price and Related Matters</b></font><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b>.</b></font></b><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font style="font-weight:normal;">&#160; In
consideration of the sale and transfer of all of Seller&#146;s rights, title and
interests in the Acquired Assets, Buyer shall assume the Assumed Liabilities
and shall pay to the Seller an aggregate purchase price of $8,700,000 (the &#147;</font></b><i><font style="font-style:italic;">Purchase Price</font></i></font><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font style="font-weight:normal;">&#148;), subject to adjustment pursuant to <u>Section 2.06</u> below.&#160; At the Closing, except as provided in <u>Section
2.07</u>, Buyer shall pay the Purchase Price to Seller by:</font></b></font></font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; wire transfer of immediately
available funds (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Cash
Payment</font></i></b>&#148;) equal to the sum of (i) $2,762,000 and (ii) the
aggregate amount of cash payments made, or to be made, by Seller to the Seller
Rights Holders in settlement of the Seller&#146;s Unit Appreciation Rights granted
pursuant to the Unit Plan, as set forth on <u>Schedule 2.05(a)</u>; and</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; a number of shares of Parent Common
Stock (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Stock
Payment</font></i></b>&#148;) equal to (i) $5,938,000, less the cash payment amount
described in <u>Section 2.05(a)(ii)</u>, and subject to adjustment pursuant to <u>Section
2.06(a)</u> and <u>Section 2.06(d)</u>, divided by (ii) (A) $3.75 if the Parent
Stock Per Share Price is equal to or less than $3.75, (B) the Parent Stock Per
Share Price if the Parent Stock Per Share Price is between $3.75 and $4.75, or
(C) $4.75 if the Parent Stock Per Share Price is equal to or greater than $4.75
(the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Applicable Stock
Price</font></i></b>&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 2.06&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="AdjustmentOfStockPayment">Adjustment
of Stock Payment</a>.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; No more than three days prior to the
Closing Date, the Seller will prepare and deliver to Buyer a calculation and
statement of its estimated Net Working Capital as of the Closing Date (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Statement</font></i></b>&#148;).&#160; The Seller will prepare the Estimated
Statement in good faith, in a manner consistent with the procedures used to
prepare the Financial Statements, subject to Buyer&#146;s review and reasonable
satisfaction.&#160; If the Net Working Capital
set forth on the Estimated Statement (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Estimated Net Working Capital</font></i></b>&#148;) is less than
$1,837,000 (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Net
Working Capital Threshold Amount</font></i></b>&#148;), then the Purchase Price and
the Stock Payment will be reduced by the amount of such deficiency.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; As soon as practicable but in no
event later than thirty (30)<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>days
following the Closing Date, Buyer will prepare and deliver to Seller a
calculation and statement of the Net Working Capital as of the Closing Date
(the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Closing Date
Statement</font></i></b>&#148;).&#160; Seller may
submit to Buyer, not later than fifteen (15)<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>days
from the receipt of the Closing Date Statement from Buyer, a list of any
components of the Closing Date Statement with which the Seller disagrees, if
any (a &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Dispute Notice</i></b></font>&#148;).&#160; If the Seller does not issue a Dispute Notice
prior to such date, the Closing Date Statement, as supplied to Seller, shall be
deemed to have been accepted and agreed to by Seller, and shall be final and
binding on the parties to this Agreement.&#160;
In the event of a Dispute Notice by the Seller, Buyer and Seller shall
thereafter for a period of up to fifteen (15) days negotiate in good faith to
resolve any items of dispute.&#160; Any items
of dispute regarding the</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Closing Date Statement which are
not so resolved shall be submitted to a mutually agreed upon certified public
accountant (the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Arbitrating Accountant</i></b></font>&#148;) or
another nationally recognized firm of public accountants mutually acceptable to
Buyer and Seller, who shall serve as an arbitrator hereunder, the expenses of
which shall be shared one-half by Buyer and one-half by Seller, unless
otherwise determined by the Arbitrating Accountant.&#160; In connection with the resolution of any dispute,
the Arbitrating Accountant shall have access to all documents, records, work
papers, facilities and personnel necessary to perform its function as
arbitrator.&#160; The Arbitrating Accountant
so selected shall render a written decision as promptly as practicable, but in
no event later than thirty (30) days after submission of the matter to the
Arbitrating Accountant.&#160; The decision of
the Arbitrating Accountant shall be final and binding upon the parties, and
judgment may be entered on such decision in a court of competent
jurisdiction.&#160; To the extent not
otherwise provided herein, the commercial arbitration rules of the American
Arbitration Association as in effect at the time of any arbitration shall
govern such arbitration in all respects.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; If the Net Working Capital, as
finally determined based upon the Closing Date Statement (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Actual Net Working Capital</font></i></b>&#148;),
is less than the lower of (A) the Net Working Capital Threshold Amount or (B)
the Estimated Net Working Capital (such shortfall, if any, referred to herein
as the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Actual Net Working Capital Shortfall</i></b></font>&#148;),
then Buyer may claim the amount of such shortfall as Damages pursuant to <u>Section
9.01</u>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; In the event that there was a
Purchase Price and Stock Payment adjustment at Closing pursuant to <u>Section
2.06(a)</u> above and the Actual Net Working Capital exceeds the Estimated Net
Working Capital, then the Purchase Price and the Stock Payment will be
increased by an amount equal to (i) the lower of (A) the Net Working Capital
Threshold and (B) the Actual Net Working Capital, less (ii) the Estimated Net
Working Capital.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 2.07&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="EscrowedShares">Escrowed Shares</a><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>.</i></b></font></font></b><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; </font></i></b></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">On the Closing Date, Buyer will withhold from the Stock Payment portion
of the Purchase Price and deposit into escrow for and on behalf of Seller a
number of shares of Parent Common Stock equal to $900,000 divided by the
Applicable Stock Price (the &#147;</font></i></b></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Escrowed

held in escrow for a period of one (1) year from the Closing Date, subject to
the provisions of Article IX hereof, pursuant to the terms and subject to the
conditions set forth in an escrow agreement to be entered into among the
parties hereto and Continental Stock Transfer &amp; Trust Company, as Escrow
Agent, in the form attached hereto as <u>Exhibit A</u>, with such modifications
as may be reasonably acceptable to Parent and Buyer, as requested by the Escrow
Agent (the &#147;</font></i></b></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Escrow
Agreement</font></i></b></font><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;">&#148;).</font></i></b></font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">2.08&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="Allocation">Allocation</a></font></b>.&#160;
Buyer and Seller agree to allocate the Purchase Price (and all other
capitalizable costs) and the Assumed Liabilities among the Acquired Assets for
all purposes (including financial accounting and tax purposes) in accordance
with the allocation schedule set forth on <u>Schedule 2.08</u> attached
hereto.&#160; Neither Buyer nor Seller shall
take any position for purposes of any federal, state or local income tax with
respect to the allocation of the Purchase Price which is inconsistent with such
allocation.</font></p>

III<br>
REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES OF SELLER</font></b></a></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Seller
represents and warrants to Parent and Buyer that the statements contained below
are true and correct, except as set forth in the disclosure schedule (the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Seller Disclosure Schedule</i></b></font>&#148;) delivered by the Seller to
Parent and Buyer, on the date hereof and as of the Closing.&#160; The disclosures in any section or subsection
of the Seller Disclosure Schedule shall qualify other sections and subsections
in this Article III where it should be reasonably apparent that such disclosure
relates to other such sections and subsections.&#160;
For purposes of this Agreement, &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Seller
Material Adverse Effect</i></b></font>&#148; shall mean a material adverse effect on
the business or financial condition of the Seller, taken as a whole.&#160; When used herein, the term &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>to the knowledge of the Seller</i></b></font>&#148; shall mean the actual
knowledge of the executive officers of the Seller.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="Corporateorganizationandqualdoc1">3.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Corporate

duly organized, validly existing and in good standing under the laws of the
State of Texas.&#160; Seller has the limited
liability company power and authority to own or lease all of its properties and
assets and to carry on its business as it is now being conducted, and is duly
licensed or qualified to do business in each jurisdiction in which the nature
of the business conducted by it or the character or location of the properties
and assets owned or leased by it makes such licensing or qualification
necessary, except where the failure to be so licensed or qualified and in good
standing would not have a Seller Material Adverse Effect.&#160; The Articles of Organization and Regulations
of Seller, copies of which have previously been delivered to Parent, are true,
accurate and complete copies of such documents as in effect as of the date of
this Agreement.</font></p>

equity interest, directly or indirectly, in any corporation, partnership,
limited liability company, association, joint venture, business trust or other
entity which is engaged in the Business.</font></p>

and in the amounts as set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Schedule 3.02</u></font>.&#160; Except as set forth in <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Schedule 3.02</u></font> hereto and <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Section 3.02(b)</u></font> hereof, the Seller does not

of preferred stock or other</font></p>

therefor exist.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 3.25&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="Disclosure">Disclosure</a>.</font></b></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; No representation or

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 3.26&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="PrivatePlacementExemption">Private

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Other than a distribution of the

Employee Stockholders in accordance with the terms of this Agreement, Seller

Common Stock (or any interest therein) in violation of applicable securities
laws.&#160; Seller understands that the shares
of Parent Common Stock so issued to Seller will not be registered under the

Act</i></b></font>&#148;) at the time of such issuance by reason of a specific

intent as expressed herein.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Seller has such knowledge and

Seller has relied upon, and is making its investment decision upon, the

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Seller is not acquiring the shares of

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><a name="ArticleIvRepresentationsAndWarrantie"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ARTICLE IV<br>
REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES OF PARENT AND BUYER</font></b></a></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Parent and Buyer hereby, jointly and severally, represent and warrant to the
Seller that the statements contained below are true and correct, except as set
forth in the disclosure schedule (the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Parent
Disclosure Schedule</i></b></font>&#148;) delivered by the Parent and Buyer to
Seller, on the date hereof and as of the Closing Date.&#160; The disclosures in any section or subsection
of the Parent Disclosure Schedule shall qualify other sections and subsections
in this Article IV where it should be reasonably apparent such disclosure
relates to other such sections and subsections.&#160;
For purposes of this Agreement, &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Parent
Material Adverse Effect</i></b></font>&#148; shall mean a material, adverse effect
on the business or financial condition of the Parent and its subsidiaries,
taken as a whole.&#160; When used herein, the
term &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>to the knowledge of the Parent</i></b></font>&#148;
shall mean the actual knowledge of the executive officers of the Parent.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 4.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="CorporateOrganizationAndQualification">Corporate Organization and
Qualification.</a></font></b></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; Each of Parent and
Buyer is a corporation duly organized, validly existing and in good standing
under the laws of the State of Delaware.&#160;
Each of Parent and Buyer has the corporate power and authority to own or
lease all of its properties and assets and to carry on its business as it is
now being conducted.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 4.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="Capitalization">Capitalization</a>.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; The authorized capital stock of
Parent consists of 40,000,000 shares of Parent Common Stock, of which

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="ArticleVCovenantsRelatingToConduct"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ARTICLE
V<br>
COVENANTS RELATING TO CONDUCT OF BUSINESS</font></b></a></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 5.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="CovenantsOfTheSeller">Covenants
of the Seller</a>.</font></b></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; During the period from the date of this
Agreement and continuing until the Closing or sooner termination of this
Agreement, except as expressly contemplated or permitted by this Agreement or
with the prior written consent of Parent, the Seller shall carry on its
business in the ordinary course consistent with past practice.&#160; The Seller shall use all reasonable efforts
to preserve its business organization, keep available the present services of
its continuing employees, continue to make regularly scheduled payments on all
of its existing debt and preserve for itself and Buyer and Parent the goodwill
of the customers of the Seller and others with whom business relationships
exist, including, but not limited to all Assigned Contracts.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 5.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="AccessToInformationConfidentiality">Access to Information; Confidentiality</a>.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Subject to <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Section
5.02(b)</u></font>, the Seller shall afford to Parent, and shall cause its
independent accountants to afford to Parent and Parent&#146;s accountants, counsel
and other representatives, reasonable access during normal business hours
during the period prior to the Closing to all of the Seller&#146;s assets,
properties, Contracts and Business Records, and the Seller shall permit Parent
and its representatives to make abstracts from and copies of such Contracts and
Business Records.&#160; During such period,
the Seller shall use its commercially reasonable efforts to furnish promptly to
Parent all other information concerning the Business, assets, properties and
personnel of the Seller as Parent may reasonably request.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; No party (or its representatives,

parties hereto agree that the remedy at law for any breach of the requirements

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 5.03&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="NoSolicitationOfTransactions">No

interests or significant assets of the Seller; or (iii) the issuance of any new

transaction.</font></p>

hand in connection with statements or omissions which resulted in such
expenses, claims, losses, damages or liabilities as well as any other relevant
equitable considerations.&#160; Relative fault
shall be determined by reference to, among other things, whether the untrue or

to state a material fact relates to information supplied by the indemnifying

access to information and opportunity to correct or prevent such untrue
statement or omission.&#160; The parties
hereto agree that it would not be just and equitable if contributions pursuant to
this paragraph were-to be determined by pro rata allocation or by any other

within the meaning of the Securities Act shall be entitled to contribution from

(ii) cause the Continuing Employees to perform services exclusively for the
benefit of the Parent (at the level and to the extent such services were
performed for the Seller prior to the Closing) from the Closing Date through
January 31, 2005 (the &#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Transition
Period</font></i></b>&#148;).&#160; During the
Transition Period, Parent will offer employment, effective no later than
February 1, 2005, to each Continuing Employee.&#160;
It shall be a condition to the employment of each Continuing Employee
with the Parent that such person execute the Parent&#146;s standard Confidentiality
and Intellectual Property Assignment Agreement in the form attached hereto as <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Exhibit H</u></font> .</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 6.06&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="EmployeeBenefitPlansAndStockOption">Employee Benefit Plans and Stock Option
Grants</a>.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Effective as of no later than
February 1, 2005, Parent shall, or shall cause its affiliates to, (i) cause
each Continuing Employee to be covered under each employee benefit plan,
program, or arrangement, including, but not limited to, any qualified
retirement, medical, dental, vision, life insurance, cafeteria, disability,
severance, nonqualified deferred compensation, or paid time-off plan,
maintained by Parent or any of its affiliates (&#147;<b><i><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Parent Plan</font></i></b>&#148;) for which such Continuing
Employee is eligible under the terms and conditions of each such Parent
Plan.&#160; With respect to such Parent Plans,
Parent shall credit prior service of the Continuing Employees with Seller as
reflected on the records of Seller provided to Parent for purposes of
participation and vesting under any such Parent Plan and for purposes of
participation, vesting, and calculation of benefits for periods after the
Closing Date with respect to vacation, sick days, severance and post-employment
benefits to the extent that such service is recognized under the analogous
benefit plans and programs maintained by or on behalf of Seller (but this
credit will not obligate Parent or Buyer to continue the employee benefit plans
and programs maintained by Parent or Buyer or otherwise alter the terms and
conditions of the Parent Plans or Parent&#146;s or Buyer&#146;s vacation, sick days,
severance and post-employment benefits or any of them); provided, that such
service need not be credited to the extent it will result in duplication of
benefits.&#160; Any pre-existing condition
restrictions and waiting period limitations that were deemed satisfied with
respect to a particular person under any Current Employee Benefit Plan that is
a group health plan immediately prior to the Closing Date shall be deemed
satisfied by Parent and Buyer under their respective group health plans with
respect to such person on or after the Closing Date to the extent (and only to
the extent) agreed to by the insurer, if any, of the applicable Parent or buyer
group health plan.&#160; The Parent shall
assume and honor, or cause the Buyer to assume and honor, all paid time-off
obligations such as vacation and sick days, to the extent that such obligations
are reflected on the Closing Date Statement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; The parties hereby agree that (i)

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><a name="ArticleViiConditionsPrecedent"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ARTICLE VII<br>
CONDITIONS PRECEDENT</font></b></a></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 7.01&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="ConditionsToEachPartysObligation">Conditions to Each Party&#146;s Obligation</a>.</font></b></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; The respective
obligation of each party under this Agreement shall be subject to the
satisfaction at or prior to the Closing of the following conditions:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Regulatory
Approvals</u></font>.&#160; All necessary
approvals, authorizations and consents of all Governmental Entities required to
consummate the transactions contemplated hereby shall have been obtained and
shall remain in full force and effect and all statutory waiting periods in
respect thereof shall have expired or been terminated (all such approvals and
the expiration of all such waiting periods being referred to herein as the &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Requisite Regulatory Approvals</i></b></font>&#148;).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>No
Injunctions or Restraints; Illegality</u></font>.&#160; No order, injunction or decree issued by any
court or agency of competent jurisdiction or other legal restraint or
prohibition (an &#147;<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"><b><i>Injunction</i></b></font>&#148;) preventing any
of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement shall be in effect and no
proceeding initiated by any Governmental Entity seeking an injunction shall be
pending.&#160; No statute, rule, regulation,
order, injunction or decree shall have been enacted, entered, promulgated or
enforced by any Governmental Entity which prohibits, restricts or makes illegal
any of the transactions contemplated by this Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 7.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="ConditionsToObligationsOfParentAnd">Conditions to Obligations of Parent and
Buyer</a></font></b></font><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">.</font></b></font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The obligation of Parent and Buyer to effect the
transactions contemplated hereby is also subject to the satisfaction or waiver
by Parent or Buyer, at or prior to the Closing, of the following conditions:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Representations
and Warranties</u></font>.&#160; The
representations and warranties of the Seller set forth in this Agreement shall
be true and correct in all material respects as of the date of this Agreement
and as of the Closing Date as though made on and as of the Closing Date (except
to the extent such representations and warranties speak as of an earlier date),
except to the extent that such representations and warranties are qualified by
the term &#147;material&#148; or contain terms such as &#147;Seller Material Adverse Effect&#148;
in which case such representations and warranties shall be true and correct in
all respects as of the date of this Agreement and at and as of the Closing Date
(except to the extent such representations and warranties speak as of an
earlier date).&#160; Parent shall receive at
Closing a certificate signed on behalf of the Seller by an authorized officer
to the foregoing effect.</font></p>

Material Adverse Changes</u></font>.&#160;
During the period between the execution of this Agreement and the
Closing Date, there shall not have been any Seller Material Adverse Effect and
no fact or condition specific to the Seller shall exist which has had or would
reasonably be expected to cause such a Seller Material Adverse Effect after the
Closing; provided, however, that for purposes of this <u>Section 7.02(p)</u>,
Seller Material Adverse Effect shall exclude any change or effect due to (i)&nbsp;the
execution and consummation of this Agreement and the transactions contemplated
hereby, (ii)&nbsp;any action taken by Seller, the Seller Interest Holders or
their respective representatives required or permitted by the terms of this
Agreement or necessary to consummate the transactions contemplated by this
Agreement, (iii)&nbsp;the general state of the industries in which the Business
operates, or (iv)&nbsp;general legal, regulatory, political, business or
economic conditions generally affecting the economy as a whole.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-weight:bold;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 7.03&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <a name="ConditionsToObligationsOfTheSeller">Conditions to Obligations of the Seller</a>.</font></b></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160; The obligations of
the Seller to effect the transactions contemplated hereby is also subject to
the satisfaction, or waiver by the Seller, at or prior to the Closing of the
following conditions:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Representations
and Warranties</u></font>.&#160; The
representations and warranties of Parent and Buyer set forth in this Agreement
shall be true and correct in all material respects as of the date of this
Agreement and as of the Closing Date as though made on and as of the Closing
Date (except to the extent such representations and warranties speak as of an
earlier date), except to the extent that such representations and warranties
are qualified by the term &#147;material&#148; or contain terms such as &#147;Parent Material
Adverse Effect&#148; in which case such representations and warranties shall be true
and correct in all respects as of the date of this Agreement and at and as of
the Closing Date (except to the extent such representations and warranties
speak as of an earlier date).&#160; The Seller
shall receive at Closing a certificate signed on behalf of Parent by an
authorized officer to the foregoing effect.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Performance
of Obligations of Parent and Buyer</u></font>.&#160;
Parent and Buyer shall have each performed all obligations required to
be performed by them under this Agreement at or prior to the Closing Date, and
the Seller shall receive at Closing a certificate signed on behalf of Parent
and Buyer by an authorized officer of each company to such effect.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Opinion of
Counsel for the Parent and Buyer</u></font>.&#160;
The Seller shall have received an opinion of counsel of Parent and Buyer
in substantially the form attached as <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Exhibit K</u></font>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>Escrow
Agreement</u></font>.&#160; The Parent, Buyer,
and the Escrow Agent shall each have executed and delivered the Escrow
Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agreement and Bill of Sale. The
Parent and Buyer shall each have executed and delivered the Agreement and Bill
of Sale.</font></u></font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Transition
Services Agreement</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160; The Parent shall have executed and delivered
the Transition Services Agreement.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <font style="text-decoration:underline;"><u>No
